===== 文件: H:\AI\AI_TOOLS\webapps\doc\docService.py =====
=== 代碼內容 ===
from __future__ import annotations

from typing import List, Any
import base64
import io

from markitdown import MarkItDown

from model.DCS1_EMAL_FILE import DCS1_EMAL_FILE

# ✅ 統一走 llm_factory（禁止在子系統 new Ollama / 自打 OpenAI HTTP）
from webapps.llm.llm_factory import get_chat_model


def _as_text(x: Any) -> str:
    """
    把 LangChain 回傳統一轉成字串（支援 AIMessage.content / 或直接 str）
    """
    if x is None:
        return ""
    if hasattr(x, "content"):
        try:
            return str(x.content or "")
        except Exception:
            pass
    return str(x)


class docService:
    def __init__(self, model: str = "mistral_small_3_1_2503:latest", *, temperature: float | None = None, timeout: int | None = None):
        """
        model 參數保留（相容舊呼叫點），但實際模型由 .env 的 OLLAMA_MODEL / OPENAI_MODEL 控制。
        若你想讓 model 真的生效，建議改成：在 llm_factory 以 env 控制，不在這裡硬塞。
        """
        self.temperature = temperature
        self.timeout = timeout
        self.llm = get_chat_model(temperature=temperature, timeout=timeout)

    def convert_to_file_list(self, json_data):
        dcsi_emal_files = [DCS1_EMAL_FILE(**item) for item in json_data]
        return dcsi_emal_files

    def summary(self, docFiles: List[DCS1_EMAL_FILE]):
        if len(docFiles) == 0:
            raise Exception("沒有來文附件可供總結")

        context: List[str] = []
        md = MarkItDown()

        for docFile in docFiles:
            # 解碼 Base64 字串
            decoded_data = base64.b64decode(docFile.EF_DATA)
            stream = io.BytesIO(decoded_data)

            md_result = md.convert_stream(stream)
            md_text = (getattr(md_result, "text_content", "") or "").strip()

            md_content = f"檔案名稱：{docFile.EF_NAME}，內容：{md_text}---"
            context.append(md_content)

        context_str = "\n".join(context)

        system_prompt = """
你是軍備局生產製造中心的公文助理，請遵守規則進行任務處理並且只能使用繁體中文回覆，另外可以參考以下資訊以協助你進行總結：
1.有意義的檔案名稱高機率代表來文的文頭，裡面的標題可以先讓你鎖定處理範圍。
2.來文的附件說明會有說明檔名的用途，你可以用這個作為檔案內容參考。
Content:
{context}
""".strip()

        html_output = """
回答時請依照以下要求：
1.用html格式輸出，請用div包住結果即可
2.不用特地告知我是使用html格式回覆
3.去除換行符號(\\n或\\\\n)，改用<br/>
4.不要在結果的頭尾出現「"」與「```」
5.開頭需要請列出發文字號與來文主旨
""".strip()

        # 你原本還有 markdown_output，但目前流程用 html_output；保留註解即可
        # markdown_output = """..."""

        # ✅ 組合成最終 prompt（直接用字串，避免不同 LLM 對 PromptValue 型別不相容）
        final_prompt = f"""{system_prompt}

{html_output}

請總結並條列出Content內的重點
""".strip().format(context=context_str)

        result = self.llm.invoke(final_prompt)
        return _as_text(result).strip()



===== 文件: H:\AI\AI_TOOLS\webapps\doc\models.py =====
=== 代碼內容 ===
from __future__ import annotations

from typing import Any, Dict, List

from django.conf import settings
from django.core.exceptions import ValidationError
from django.db import models
from django.db.models import Q

# ============================================================
# New schema rules (system format)
# ============================================================

DOC_TYPE_CHOICES = [
    ("sign_memo", "簽呈"),
    ("order_draft", "令稿"),
    ("submit_draft", "呈稿"),
    ("letter_draft", "函稿"),
    ("note", "便籤"),
]

SCOPE_CHOICES = [
    ("public", "公開"),
    ("personal", "個人"),
]

DOC_TYPE_SECTION_RULES: Dict[str, Dict[str, List[str]]] = {
    "sign_memo": {
        "required": ["subject", "explain", "method"],
        "optional": ["attachments", "closing", "recipients"],
    },
    "submit_draft": {
        "required": ["subject", "explain"],
        "optional": ["method", "attachments", "closing", "recipients"],
    },
    "order_draft": {
        "required": ["subject", "explain"],
        "optional": ["enforce", "attachments", "recipients", "closing"],
    },
    "letter_draft": {
        "required": ["subject", "explain"],
        "optional": ["method", "attachments", "closing", "recipients"],
    },
    "note": {
        "required": ["title", "points"],
        "optional": ["action", "owner", "due", "ref"],
    },
}

LETTER_DOC_FIELDS_DEFAULT: Dict[str, Any] = {
    "recipient_name": "",
    "recipient_zip": "",
    "recipient_address": "",
    "publish_date": "",
    "show_publish_date": False,
}


def _s(v: Any) -> str:
    return ("" if v is None else str(v)).strip()


def _list_str(v: Any) -> List[str]:
    if isinstance(v, list):
        out: List[str] = []
        seen = set()
        for x in v:
            s = _s(x)
            if s and s not in seen:
                seen.add(s)
                out.append(s)
        return out
    return []


def _dict(v: Any) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    return v if isinstance(v, dict) else {}


class DocumentTemplate(models.Model):
    """
    新制模板：
    - sections: 結構化段落
    - doc_fields: 函稿常用欄位
    - content_text: 預覽/全文檢索/匯出用（可由 sections 合成，但不強制覆寫）
    """

    # ✅ 讓外部（views / seed / 管理指令）可穩定引用
    DOC_TYPE_CHOICES = DOC_TYPE_CHOICES
    SCOPE_CHOICES = SCOPE_CHOICES
    DOC_TYPE_SECTION_RULES = DOC_TYPE_SECTION_RULES
    LETTER_DOC_FIELDS_DEFAULT = LETTER_DOC_FIELDS_DEFAULT

    title = models.CharField(max_length=200, db_index=True)
    doc_type = models.CharField(max_length=40, choices=DOC_TYPE_CHOICES, db_index=True)
    description = models.CharField(max_length=400, blank=True, default="")

    sections = models.JSONField(default=dict, blank=True)
    doc_fields = models.JSONField(default=dict, blank=True)

    schema_ver = models.PositiveSmallIntegerField(default=2, db_index=True)
    meta = models.JSONField(default=dict, blank=True)

    # ✅ 可直接存「全文型範例」；若 sections 有內容才會重建
    content_text = models.TextField(blank=True, default="")

    tags = models.JSONField(default=list, blank=True)

    scope = models.CharField(
        max_length=20,
        choices=SCOPE_CHOICES,
        default="public",
        db_index=True,
    )
    owner = models.ForeignKey(
        settings.AUTH_USER_MODEL,
        null=True,
        blank=True,
        on_delete=models.CASCADE,
        related_name="doc_templates",
        db_index=True,
    )

    created_at = models.DateTimeField(auto_now_add=True, db_index=True)
    updated_at = models.DateTimeField(auto_now=True, db_index=True)

    class Meta:
        indexes = [
            models.Index(fields=["doc_type", "scope", "created_at"], name="idx_doc_type_scope_created"),
            models.Index(fields=["schema_ver", "doc_type"], name="idx_doc_schema_doctype"),
        ]
        constraints = [
            models.UniqueConstraint(
                fields=["title"],
                condition=Q(scope="public"),
                name="uniq_doc_template_public_title",
            ),
            models.UniqueConstraint(
                fields=["owner", "title"],
                condition=Q(scope="personal") & Q(owner__isnull=False),
                name="uniq_doc_template_personal_owner_title",
            ),
        ]

    def __str__(self) -> str:
        return f"{self.get_doc_type_display()} | {self.title}"

    # ------------------------------------------------------------
    # Validation
    # ------------------------------------------------------------
    def clean(self) -> None:
        super().clean()

        # 1) doc_type 必須合法
        dt = _s(self.doc_type)
        valid_types = {k for k, _ in DOC_TYPE_CHOICES}
        if dt not in valid_types:
            raise ValidationError({"doc_type": f"Invalid doc_type: {dt}"})

        # 2) scope / owner 一致性（避免髒資料）
        sc = _s(self.scope) or "public"
        if sc not in {k for k, _ in SCOPE_CHOICES}:
            raise ValidationError({"scope": f"Invalid scope: {sc}"})

        if sc == "public":
            # 公開模板不應綁 owner（避免誤判權限）
            if self.owner_id is not None:
                self.owner = None
        elif sc == "personal":
            # 個人模板必須有 owner
            if self.owner_id is None:
                raise ValidationError({"owner": "personal scope requires owner"})

        # 3) JSON 欄位型別正規化
        self.tags = _list_str(self.tags)
        self.sections = _dict(self.sections)
        self.doc_fields = _dict(self.doc_fields)
        self.meta = _dict(self.meta)

        # 4) sections 規則檢查（若 rules 不存在就跳過）
        rules = DOC_TYPE_SECTION_RULES.get(dt)
        if not rules:
            return

        # note 規則
        if dt == "note":
            title = _s(self.sections.get("title"))
            if not title:
                raise ValidationError({"sections": "note.sections.title is required"})

            pts = self.sections.get("points")
            if not isinstance(pts, list):
                raise ValidationError({"sections": "note.sections.points must be a list"})

            pts_clean = [_s(p) for p in pts if _s(p)]
            if not pts_clean:
                raise ValidationError({"sections": "note.sections.points must be a non-empty list"})

            # ✅ 讓資料更乾淨：把 points 清成乾淨 list（可選，但很實用）
            self.sections["points"] = pts_clean

            # note 不強制 content_text/sections 之外的欄位
            return

        # 一般公文規則（required 欄位都要非空）
        req = set(rules.get("required", []))
        missing = []
        for k in req:
            v = self.sections.get(k)
            if not _s(v):
                missing.append(k)
        if missing:
            raise ValidationError({"sections": f"Missing required sections: {', '.join(missing)}"})

        # 函稿預設欄位補齊（只在 letter_draft）
        if dt == "letter_draft":
            if not self.doc_fields:
                self.doc_fields = {}
            for k, dv in LETTER_DOC_FIELDS_DEFAULT.items():
                self.doc_fields.setdefault(k, dv)

    # ------------------------------------------------------------
    # Build content_text from sections
    # ------------------------------------------------------------
    def build_content_text(self) -> str:
        dt = _s(self.doc_type)
        s = _dict(self.sections)

        if dt == "note":
            title = _s(s.get("title"))
            pts = s.get("points") if isinstance(s.get("points"), list) else []
            pts2 = [f"• {_s(p)}" for p in pts if _s(p)]
            action = _s(s.get("action"))

            lines: List[str] = []
            if title:
                lines.append(f"主旨：{title}")
            if pts2:
                lines.append("重點：")
                lines.extend(pts2)
            if action:
                lines.append(f"擬辦：{action}")
            return "\n".join(lines).strip()

        subject = _s(s.get("subject"))
        explain = _s(s.get("explain"))
        method = _s(s.get("method"))
        attachments = _s(s.get("attachments"))
        closing = _s(s.get("closing"))
        enforce = _s(s.get("enforce"))

        lines: List[str] = []
        if subject:
            lines.append(f"主旨：{subject}")

        if explain:
            lines.append("說明：")
            lines.append(explain)

        if dt == "order_draft":
            if enforce:
                lines.append("施行：")
                lines.append(enforce)
        else:
            if method:
                lines.append("擬辦：")
                lines.append(method)

        if attachments:
            lines.append("附件：")
            lines.append(attachments)

        # 函稿 closing 才直接附在最後
        if closing and dt == "letter_draft":
            lines.append(closing)

        return "\n".join([x for x in lines if _s(x)]).strip()

    # ------------------------------------------------------------
    # Save override
    # ------------------------------------------------------------
    def save(self, *args, **kwargs) -> None:
        """
        ✅ 必修：不要無條件覆寫 content_text
        - 若是「全文型範例」(只填 content_text)，sections 可能是 {}
          -> 必須保留 content_text 原文，不要重組
        - 若 sections 有內容（結構化模板），才用 build_content_text 重建預覽全文
        """
        try:
            if isinstance(self.sections, dict) and self.sections:
                self.content_text = self.build_content_text()
        except Exception:
            # 任何 build 失敗都不要影響存檔
            pass

        super().save(*args, **kwargs)



===== 文件: H:\AI\AI_TOOLS\webapps\doc\prompt.py =====
=== 代碼內容 ===
# webapps/doc/prompt.py
from __future__ import annotations

import os
from typing import Optional, List, Dict, Set


# ============================================================
# New-only doc type spec (no legacy compatibility)
# ============================================================

ALLOWED_DOC_TYPES: Set[str] = {"sign_memo", "order_draft", "submit_draft", "letter_draft", "note"}

DOC_TYPE_LABEL: Dict[str, str] = {
    "sign_memo": "簽呈",
    "order_draft": "令稿",
    "submit_draft": "呈稿",
    "letter_draft": "函稿",
    "note": "便籤",
}


def _env_bool(k: str, d: bool = False) -> bool:
    v = (os.getenv(k) or "").strip().lower()
    if not v:
        return d
    return v in ("1", "true", "yes", "y", "on")


# ✅ 開發/測試想嚴格一點：PROMPT_STRICT_DOCTYPE=1
_PROMPT_STRICT_DOCTYPE = _env_bool("PROMPT_STRICT_DOCTYPE", False)


def normalize_doc_type(doc_type: str) -> str:
    """
    新制：只允許固定 doc_type。
    - 預設：不合法 doc_type fallback 成 submit_draft（避免前端送錯導致 prompt 走偏）
    - 嚴格模式（PROMPT_STRICT_DOCTYPE=1）：直接 raise ValueError（方便抓 bug）
    """
    dt = (doc_type or "").strip()
    if dt in ALLOWED_DOC_TYPES:
        return dt
    if _PROMPT_STRICT_DOCTYPE:
        raise ValueError(f"invalid doc_type: {dt!r}, allowed={sorted(ALLOWED_DOC_TYPES)}")
    return "submit_draft"


def doc_type_label(doc_type: str) -> str:
    dt = normalize_doc_type(doc_type)
    return DOC_TYPE_LABEL.get(dt, "公文")


def format_guide_by_doc_type(doc_type: str) -> str:
    dt = normalize_doc_type(doc_type)

    if dt == "sign_memo":  # 簽呈
        return (
            "格式建議（簽呈）：\n"
            "1) 主旨：一句話說明要核定/同意/辦理的事項。\n"
            "2) 說明：列點交代背景、依據、現況、必要性、影響與風險（可含附件）。\n"
            "3) 擬辦：列點寫具體辦法、期程、分工、經費與風險控管。\n"
            "4) 附件：若有附件，列出附件名稱或摘要。\n"
        )

    if dt == "order_draft":  # 令稿
        return (
            "格式建議（令稿）：\n"
            "1) 主旨：清楚宣示公告/通知/命令事項（含生效日）。\n"
            "2) 說明：條列適用範圍、作業內容、配合事項、窗口與期限。\n"
            "3) 施行：若有過渡期/生效日/廢止或修正重點，請寫明。\n"
        )

    if dt == "submit_draft":  # 呈稿
        return (
            "格式建議（呈稿）：\n"
            "1) 主旨：概述呈報事項與請示結論。\n"
            "2) 說明：背景、依據、現況與問題點（可條列）。\n"
            "3) 建議/請示：提出可執行方案、請核示事項、期程與資源需求。\n"
            "4) 附件：若有附件，列出附件名稱或摘要。\n"
        )

    if dt == "letter_draft":  # 函稿
        return (
            "格式建議（函稿）：\n"
            "1) 主旨：說明函復/函請事項。\n"
            "2) 說明：交代依據、事由、辦理情形或請求事項（可條列）。\n"
            "3) 辦法/配合：需對方回覆或配合事項，請列出期限與方式。\n"
            "4) 附件：若有附件，列出附件名稱或摘要。\n"
            "5) 結語：常用『請查照』『請惠復』『特此函達』擇一。\n"
        )

    if dt == "note":  # 便籤
        return (
            "格式建議（便籤）：\n"
            "1) 主旨：一句話說明要點。\n"
            "2) 重點：條列 3~7 點（背景/現況/待辦/期限/承辦）。\n"
            "3) 擬辦/請示：需要請示/請協助/請知悉的結尾。\n"
        )

    # fallback (shouldn't happen)
    return (
        "格式建議：\n"
        "1) 主旨\n"
        "2) 說明\n"
        "3) 擬辦\n"
        "4) 附件（如有）\n"
    )


def hard_rules(doc_type: str) -> str:
    dt = normalize_doc_type(doc_type)

    if dt == "letter_draft":
        section_rule = "主旨／說明／辦法(或配合事項)／附件(如有)／結語(如：請查照)。"
    elif dt == "order_draft":
        section_rule = "主旨／說明／施行(生效日或注意事項)。"
    elif dt == "note":
        section_rule = "主旨／重點／擬辦(或請示)。"
    else:
        section_rule = "主旨／說明／擬辦(或建議/請示)／附件(如有)。"

    return (
        "硬性規則：\n"
        "1) 只輸出公文『本文』，不要加任何說明、標註、前言、AI 字樣或 Markdown。\n"
        "2) 不得直接複製參考前案/範例內容，但可吸收語氣與結構。\n"
        "3) 若資料不足，請用『不臆測』原則：避免捏造日期、金額、單位名稱、文號；必要時用「○○」保留。\n"
        "4) 不要輸出機關地址、發文字號、密等、速別等抬頭欄位（除非需求明確要求寫入本文）。\n"
        f"5) 內文段落請使用：{section_rule}\n"
    )


def default_structured_output(doc_type: str) -> bool:
    dt = normalize_doc_type(doc_type)
    # ✅ 簽呈/呈稿/函稿：強制標籤較利於後端 split
    # ✅ 令稿/便籤：預設不強制，避免硬塞附件/擬辦
    return dt in {"sign_memo", "submit_draft", "letter_draft"}


def output_mode_hint(doc_type: str, structured: bool) -> str:
    if not structured:
        return ""

    dt = normalize_doc_type(doc_type)

    if dt == "letter_draft":
        return (
            "輸出格式要求（結構化）：\n"
            "- 請依序輸出並保留段落標籤：\n"
            "主旨：...\n"
            "說明：...\n"
            "辦法：...\n"
            "附件：...（若無附件，請寫「附件：無」）\n"
            "結語：...（例：請查照/請惠復/特此函達，擇一）\n"
        )

    if dt == "order_draft":
        return (
            "輸出格式要求（結構化）：\n"
            "- 請依序輸出並保留段落標籤：\n"
            "主旨：...\n"
            "說明：...\n"
            "施行：...（生效日/注意事項/過渡期）\n"
        )

    if dt == "note":
        return (
            "輸出格式要求（結構化）：\n"
            "- 請依序輸出並保留段落標籤：\n"
            "主旨：...\n"
            "重點：...\n"
            "擬辦：...\n"
        )

    # sign_memo / submit_draft
    return (
        "輸出格式要求（結構化）：\n"
        "- 請依序輸出並保留段落標籤：\n"
        "主旨：...\n"
        "說明：...\n"
        "擬辦：...\n"
        "附件：...（若無附件，請寫「附件：無」）\n"
    )


def build_prompt(
    doc_type: str,
    requirement: str,
    examples: Optional[List[str]] = None,
    reference_text: Optional[str] = None,
    incoming_text: Optional[str] = None,
    attachments_text: Optional[str] = None,
    structured_output: Optional[bool] = None,
) -> str:
    """
    新制公文草稿 Prompt Builder
    - doc_type 僅支援：sign_memo / order_draft / submit_draft / letter_draft / note
    - structured_output:
        - None：依 doc_type 自動決定
        - True：強制輸出段落標籤（利於後端 split）
        - False：不強制
    """
    examples = examples or []

    dt = normalize_doc_type(doc_type)
    label = doc_type_label(dt)
    guide = format_guide_by_doc_type(dt)

    if structured_output is None:
        structured_output = default_structured_output(dt)

    req = (requirement or "").strip()
    if not req:
        # ✅ 防呆：避免空需求還硬產 prompt
        req = "（未提供具體需求；請依既有資訊產出合理且保守的草稿，資料不足處以○○保留，不得臆測。）"

    inc = (incoming_text or "").strip()
    att = (attachments_text or "").strip()
    ref = (reference_text or "").strip()

    parts: List[str] = []
    parts.append("你是一位熟悉政府機關與公營事業公文格式的專業撰稿人員。")
    parts.append(f"請依下列資訊撰寫一份正式的「{label}」公文草稿。")

    parts.append(hard_rules(dt))

    parts.append("【格式與結構提示】")
    parts.append(guide)

    if structured_output:
        parts.append("【輸出格式要求】")
        parts.append(output_mode_hint(dt, structured=True))

    if inc:
        parts.append("【來文內容（擬案依據，請吸收重點但不得照抄）】")
        parts.append(inc)

    if att:
        parts.append("【附件內容（擬案依據，請吸收重點但不得照抄）】")
        parts.append(att)

    if ref:
        parts.append("【參考前案（請模仿語氣／結構，不得照抄）】")
        parts.append(ref)

    ex_blocks: List[str] = []
    for i, ex in enumerate(examples, 1):
        ex_text = (ex or "").strip()
        if ex_text:
            ex_blocks.append(f"（範例 {i}）\n{ex_text}")

    if ex_blocks:
        parts.append("【範例公文參考（請模仿語氣／結構，不得照抄）】")
        parts.extend(ex_blocks)

    parts.append("【本次需求說明】")
    parts.append(req)

    parts.append("【請產出完整草稿】")

    return "\n\n".join([p for p in parts if p and str(p).strip()])



===== 文件: H:\AI\AI_TOOLS\webapps\doc\sybase_incoming.py =====
=== 代碼內容 ===
# webapps/doc/sybase_incoming.py
from __future__ import annotations

import base64
import json
import mimetypes
import re
from typing import Any, Dict, List, Optional, Tuple, Sequence
from urllib.parse import quote

from django.http import HttpRequest, HttpResponse, JsonResponse
from django.views.decorators.csrf import csrf_exempt

from webapps.portal.decorators import require_node
from webapps.doc.utils_login import get_login_user_idno

# ✅ DBFactory（集中連線）— 禁止 fallback
from webapps.database.db_factory import db_query_all, db_query_one


# ============================================================
# SQL
# ✅ 注意：pyodbc placeholder 必須用 ?
# 條件：
# - 只用 TM.TM_GRSNO
# - 強制 TM_PSID = login_user
# ============================================================

SYB_INCOMING_LOOKUP_SQL = """
SELECT TOP 60
    TM.TM_GRSNO,
    TM.TM_PSID,
    TM.TM_RSTP,
    TD.TD_SUBJ,
    TD.TD_FORMAT,
    EF.EF_ID,
    EF.EF_NAME,
    TD.TD_PATH
FROM mnda.dbo.DCS3_TRST_MST TM
LEFT JOIN mnda.dbo.DCS3_TRST_DAT TD ON TM.TM_SNO = TD.TD_SNO
LEFT JOIN mnda.dbo.DCS1_EMAL_TMP EM ON TM.TM_GRSNO = EM.EM_GRSNO
LEFT JOIN mnda.dbo.DCS1_EMAL_FILE EF ON EM.EM_FID = EF.EF_ID
WHERE 1=1
  AND TM.TM_PSID = ?
  AND TM.TM_GRSNO = ?
ORDER BY TM.TM_GRSNO DESC
"""

SYB_FILE_BY_EF_ID_SQL = """
SELECT EF.EF_NAME, EF.EF_DATA
FROM mnda.dbo.DCS1_EMAL_FILE EF
WHERE CONVERT(VARCHAR(64), EF.EF_ID) = ?
"""

SYB_FILE_BY_DF_PATH_SQL = """
SELECT DF.DF_NAME, DF.DF_DATA
FROM mnda.dbo.DCS0_DOC_FILE DF
WHERE DF.DF_PATH = ?
"""

SYB_ATTACH_OWNERSHIP_EF_SQL = """
SELECT TOP 1 1
FROM mnda.dbo.DCS3_TRST_MST TM
LEFT JOIN mnda.dbo.DCS1_EMAL_TMP EM ON TM.TM_GRSNO = EM.EM_GRSNO
LEFT JOIN mnda.dbo.DCS1_EMAL_FILE EF ON EM.EM_FID = EF.EF_ID
WHERE TM.TM_PSID = ?
  AND CONVERT(VARCHAR(64), EF.EF_ID) = ?
"""

SYB_ATTACH_OWNERSHIP_DF_SQL = """
SELECT TOP 1 1
FROM mnda.dbo.DCS3_TRST_MST TM
LEFT JOIN mnda.dbo.DCS3_TRST_DAT TD ON TM.TM_SNO = TD.TD_SNO
WHERE TM.TM_PSID = ?
  AND TD.TD_PATH = ?
"""


# ============================================================
# helpers
# ============================================================

def _safe_str(x: Any) -> str:
    return "" if x is None else str(x)


def _bytes_from_blob(x: Any) -> bytes:
    if x is None:
        return b""
    if isinstance(x, bytes):
        return x
    if isinstance(x, bytearray):
        return bytes(x)
    if isinstance(x, memoryview):
        return x.tobytes()
    try:
        return bytes(x)
    except Exception:
        return b""


def _set_attachment_headers(resp: HttpResponse, filename: str) -> None:
    """
    ✅ 支援中文檔名：同時給 filename + filename*（RFC5987）
    """
    name = (filename or "").strip() or "attachment.bin"

    # ASCII fallback：避免某些 client/代理對中文 filename 不友善
    ascii_fallback = "attachment.bin"
    quoted = quote(name, safe="")
    resp["Content-Disposition"] = f'attachment; filename="{ascii_fallback}"; filename*=UTF-8\'\'{quoted}'


def _syb_query_all(sql: str, params: Sequence[Any]) -> List[Tuple]:
    # ✅ db_factory(pyodbc) 規則：params 必須 positional list/tuple，不可 dict
    return db_query_all("sybase", sql, list(params))


def _syb_query_one(sql: str, params: Sequence[Any]) -> Optional[Tuple]:
    return db_query_one("sybase", sql, list(params))


def _b64url_encode(s: str) -> str:
    raw = (s or "").encode("utf-8", errors="ignore")
    return base64.urlsafe_b64encode(raw).decode("ascii").rstrip("=")


def _b64url_decode(s: str) -> str:
    t = (s or "").strip()
    if not t:
        return ""
    pad = "=" * ((4 - (len(t) % 4)) % 4)
    try:
        return base64.urlsafe_b64decode((t + pad).encode("ascii")).decode("utf-8", errors="ignore")
    except Exception:
        return ""


def _pick_attachment_source(tm_rstp: str, td_format: str, ef_id: str, td_path: str) -> str:
    """
    依 raw_query 判斷：
      CASE WHEN TD_FORMAT not in ('檔案','來文(檔案)') AND TM_RSTP NOT IN ('創','會')
           THEN EF
           ELSE DF
    """
    fmt = (td_format or "").strip()
    rstp = (tm_rstp or "").strip()
    ef_id = (ef_id or "").strip()
    td_path = (td_path or "").strip()

    use_ef = (fmt not in ("檔案", "來文(檔案)")) and (rstp not in ("創", "會")) and bool(ef_id)
    if use_ef:
        return "EF"
    if td_path:
        return "DF"
    return "EF" if ef_id else "DF"


def _make_attach_key(kind: str, ef_id: str, td_path: str) -> str:
    if kind == "EF":
        return f"EF:{(ef_id or '').strip()}"
    return f"DF:{_b64url_encode(td_path or '')}"


def _parse_attach_key(attach_key: str) -> Tuple[str, str]:
    s = (attach_key or "").strip()
    if s.startswith("EF:"):
        return "EF", s[3:].strip()
    if s.startswith("DF:"):
        return "DF", s[3:].strip()
    # 相容舊資料：沒 prefix 就當 EF_ID
    return "EF", s


def _norm_filename(name: str) -> str:
    s = (name or "").strip()
    s = re.sub(r"\s+", " ", s)
    return s.lower()


def _dedupe_safe_filename(
    existing_norms: set,
    base_name: str,
    source: str,
    counter: Dict[Tuple[str, str], int],
) -> str:
    """
    如果同 source + filename_norm 已出現 → 改名顯示：檔名（2）（3）...
    """
    base = (base_name or "附件").strip() or "附件"
    norm = _norm_filename(base)
    k = (source, norm)

    if k not in existing_norms:
        existing_norms.add(k)
        counter[k] = 1
        return base

    n = int(counter.get(k, 1)) + 1
    counter[k] = n

    m = re.match(r"^(.*?)(\.[A-Za-z0-9]{1,10})$", base)
    if m:
        stem, ext = m.group(1), m.group(2)
        return f"{stem}（{n}）{ext}"
    return f"{base}（{n}）"


def _guess_content_type(filename: str) -> str:
    ctype, _ = mimetypes.guess_type(filename or "")
    return ctype or "application/octet-stream"


def _get_tm_grsno(request: HttpRequest) -> str:
    """
    ✅ 同時支援：
    - GET: ?tm_grsno=... 或 ?grsno=...
    - POST JSON: {"tm_grsno": "..."}
    """
    # GET first (for your current JS)
    tm_grsno = (_safe_str(request.GET.get("tm_grsno")) or "").strip()
    if not tm_grsno:
        tm_grsno = (_safe_str(request.GET.get("grsno")) or "").strip()
    if tm_grsno:
        return tm_grsno

    # POST JSON
    try:
        payload = json.loads((request.body or b"").decode("utf-8") or "{}")
    except Exception:
        payload = {}

    return (_safe_str(payload.get("tm_grsno")) or "").strip()


def _build_items_from_rows(rows: List[Tuple]) -> List[Dict[str, Any]]:
    """
    把查詢結果聚合成 items（每個案件一筆，內含 attachments）
    """
    bucket: Dict[str, Dict[str, Any]] = {}

    for r in rows or []:
        tm_grsno_v = _safe_str(r[0]).strip() if len(r) > 0 else ""
        tm_psid_v  = _safe_str(r[1]).strip() if len(r) > 1 else ""
        tm_rstp    = _safe_str(r[2]).strip() if len(r) > 2 else ""
        td_subj    = _safe_str(r[3]).strip() if len(r) > 3 else ""
        td_format  = _safe_str(r[4]).strip() if len(r) > 4 else ""
        ef_id      = _safe_str(r[5]).strip() if len(r) > 5 else ""
        ef_name    = _safe_str(r[6]).strip() if len(r) > 6 else ""
        td_path    = _safe_str(r[7]).strip() if len(r) > 7 else ""

        key = f"{tm_grsno_v}||{tm_psid_v}"
        if key not in bucket:
            bucket[key] = {
                "tm_grsno": tm_grsno_v,
                "tm_psid": tm_psid_v,
                "td_subj": td_subj,
                "attachments": [],
                "_seen_attach": set(),
                "_seen_name": set(),
                "_name_counter": {},
            }
        else:
            if not bucket[key].get("td_subj") and td_subj:
                bucket[key]["td_subj"] = td_subj

        source = _pick_attachment_source(tm_rstp, td_format, ef_id, td_path)

        if source == "EF" and not ef_id:
            continue
        if source == "DF" and not td_path:
            continue

        attach_key = _make_attach_key(source, ef_id, td_path)
        if attach_key in bucket[key]["_seen_attach"]:
            continue
        bucket[key]["_seen_attach"].add(attach_key)

        if source == "EF":
            filename = ef_name or td_subj or ef_id or "附件"
        else:
            filename = td_subj or "附件"

        filename = _dedupe_safe_filename(
            bucket[key]["_seen_name"],
            filename,
            source,
            bucket[key]["_name_counter"],
        )

        bucket[key]["attachments"].append(
            {
                "attach_key": attach_key,
                "filename": filename,
                "td_format": td_format,
                "source": source,
            }
        )

    out: List[Dict[str, Any]] = []
    for v in bucket.values():
        v.pop("_seen_attach", None)
        v.pop("_seen_name", None)
        v.pop("_name_counter", None)
        out.append(v)

    out.sort(key=lambda x: (x.get("tm_grsno", ""), x.get("td_subj", "")), reverse=True)
    return out


# ============================================================
# API
# ============================================================

@csrf_exempt
@require_node("doc", api=True)
@csrf_exempt
@require_node("doc", api=True)
def incoming_lookup(request: HttpRequest):
    """
    ✅ 支援 GET / POST
    GET:
      /doc/incoming_lookup/?tm_grsno=1150001261
    POST JSON:
      { "tm_grsno": "1150001261" }
    POST form:
      tm_grsno=1150001261

    Response:
      { ok, items: [ {tm_grsno, tm_psid, td_subj, attachments:[...]} ] }
    """
    if request.method not in ("GET", "POST"):
        return JsonResponse({"ok": False, "error": "method not allowed"}, status=405)

    # -------------------------
    # 1) login_user（強制本人承辦）
    # -------------------------
    login_user = (get_login_user_idno(request) or "").strip()
    if not login_user:
        # ✅ 讓你在 log 一眼就知道「為何 401」
        # - 本機沒有 IIS RemoteUser 時，就是靠 utils_login 的 DEV fallback
        # - 若你忘了設 DEV_LOGIN_USER / DJANGO_DEBUG，就會在這裡被擋
        return JsonResponse(
            {
                "ok": False,
                "error": "missing login_user",
                "hint": "請確認 IIS RemoteUser 是否有帶入，或本機開發已設定 DEV_LOGIN_USER（且 DJANGO_DEBUG=1）",
            },
            status=401,
        )

    # -------------------------
    # 2) tm_grsno 取得（更穩：GET / JSON / form 都支援）
    # -------------------------
    tm_grsno = _get_tm_grsno(request)

    # 也支援一般 form POST：request.POST.get(...)
    if not tm_grsno and request.method == "POST":
        try:
            tm_grsno = (_safe_str(request.POST.get("tm_grsno")) or "").strip()
            if not tm_grsno:
                tm_grsno = (_safe_str(request.POST.get("grsno")) or "").strip()
        except Exception:
            pass

    # 最後保險：去掉空白
    tm_grsno = (tm_grsno or "").strip()

    if not tm_grsno:
        return JsonResponse({"ok": False, "error": "need tm_grsno"}, status=400)

    # （可選）基本格式檢查：你範例是數字，若你確定一定是數字可保留
    # 若可能含字母，就把這段拿掉
    if not re.fullmatch(r"[0-9]{6,20}", tm_grsno):
        return JsonResponse(
            {"ok": False, "error": "invalid tm_grsno format", "tm_grsno": tm_grsno},
            status=400,
        )

    # -------------------------
    # 3) 查 Sybase
    # -------------------------
    try:
        rows = _syb_query_all(SYB_INCOMING_LOOKUP_SQL, [login_user, tm_grsno])
    except Exception as e:
        return JsonResponse(
            {
                "ok": False,
                "error": "sybase query failed",
                "detail": str(e),
                "meta": {"login_user": login_user, "tm_grsno": tm_grsno},
            },
            status=500,
        )

    items = _build_items_from_rows(rows)

    # ✅ 回傳時也帶 meta，方便你前端/Network 一眼確認「到底用哪個 login_user 去查」
    return JsonResponse(
        {"ok": True, "items": items, "meta": {"login_user": login_user, "tm_grsno": tm_grsno}},
        status=200,
    )


@csrf_exempt
@require_node("doc", api=True)
def incoming_files(request: HttpRequest):
    """
    ✅ 支援 GET / POST
    目的：提供「附件清單」獨立 API，讓前端選取某筆後可以重新抓附件（或只要拿附件 list）

    GET:
      /doc/incoming_files/?tm_grsno=1150001261
    POST JSON:
      { "tm_grsno": "1150001261" }

    Response:
      { ok, tm_grsno, attachments:[...], items:[...] }

    - attachments：把所有 items 裡的 attachments 攤平成一份（去重）
    - items：保留原本聚合結果，方便你前端若還要顯示主旨/案件
    """
    if request.method not in ("GET", "POST"):
        return JsonResponse({"ok": False, "error": "method not allowed"}, status=405)

    login_user = get_login_user_idno(request)
    if not login_user:
        return JsonResponse({"ok": False, "error": "missing login_user"}, status=401)

    tm_grsno = _get_tm_grsno(request)
    if not tm_grsno:
        return JsonResponse({"ok": False, "error": "need tm_grsno"}, status=400)

    try:
        rows = _syb_query_all(SYB_INCOMING_LOOKUP_SQL, [login_user, tm_grsno])
    except Exception as e:
        return JsonResponse({"ok": False, "error": "sybase query failed", "detail": str(e)}, status=500)

    items = _build_items_from_rows(rows)

    flat: List[Dict[str, Any]] = []
    seen = set()
    for it in items:
        for a in (it.get("attachments") or []):
            k = (_safe_str(a.get("attach_key")) or "").strip()
            if not k or k in seen:
                continue
            seen.add(k)
            flat.append(a)

    return JsonResponse({"ok": True, "tm_grsno": tm_grsno, "attachments": flat, "items": items}, status=200)


@csrf_exempt
@require_node("doc", api=True)
def incoming_file(request: HttpRequest, attach_key: str):
    """
    GET /doc/incoming_file/<attach_key>/

    - 權限驗證：attach_key 必須屬於 login_user 承辦案件
    - EF: DCS1_EMAL_FILE(EF_ID)
    - DF: DCS0_DOC_FILE(DF_PATH)（attach_key 內是 base64url 編碼的 TD_PATH）
    """
    login_user = get_login_user_idno(request)
    if not login_user:
        return JsonResponse({"ok": False, "error": "missing login_user"}, status=401)

    attach_key = (attach_key or "").strip()
    if not attach_key:
        return JsonResponse({"ok": False, "error": "empty attach_key"}, status=400)

    kind, val = _parse_attach_key(attach_key)
    if not val:
        return JsonResponse({"ok": False, "error": "invalid attach_key"}, status=400)

    try:
        if kind == "EF":
            ok = _syb_query_one(SYB_ATTACH_OWNERSHIP_EF_SQL, [login_user, val])
            if not ok:
                return JsonResponse({"ok": False, "error": "not found"}, status=404)

            row = _syb_query_one(SYB_FILE_BY_EF_ID_SQL, [val])
            if not row:
                return JsonResponse({"ok": False, "error": "not found"}, status=404)

            filename = (_safe_str(row[0]) or "attachment.bin").strip() or "attachment.bin"
            data = _bytes_from_blob(row[1] if len(row) > 1 else None)
            if not data:
                return JsonResponse({"ok": False, "error": "EF_DATA is null/empty"}, status=404)

            resp = HttpResponse(data, content_type=_guess_content_type(filename))
            _set_attachment_headers(resp, filename)
            return resp

        # DF
        df_path = _b64url_decode(val)
        if not df_path:
            return JsonResponse({"ok": False, "error": "invalid DF path"}, status=400)

        ok = _syb_query_one(SYB_ATTACH_OWNERSHIP_DF_SQL, [login_user, df_path])
        if not ok:
            return JsonResponse({"ok": False, "error": "not found"}, status=404)

        row = _syb_query_one(SYB_FILE_BY_DF_PATH_SQL, [df_path])
        if not row:
            return JsonResponse({"ok": False, "error": "not found"}, status=404)

        filename = (_safe_str(row[0]) or "attachment.bin").strip() or "attachment.bin"
        data = _bytes_from_blob(row[1] if len(row) > 1 else None)
        if not data:
            return JsonResponse({"ok": False, "error": "DF_DATA is null/empty"}, status=404)

        resp = HttpResponse(data, content_type=_guess_content_type(filename))
        _set_attachment_headers(resp, filename)
        return resp

    except Exception as e:
        return JsonResponse({"ok": False, "error": "sybase download failed", "detail": str(e)}, status=500)

# webapps/doc/urls.py
from __future__ import annotations

from django.urls import path

from webapps.doc.views_sybase_blob import (
    api_sybase_blob_download,
    api_sybase_blob_stash,
)
from . import views

# ============================================================
# 規範註解（Mandatory）
# 1) urls.py 路徑不得包含 proxy prefix（例如 /djangoai、/comment 等）
#    - 反向代理 prefix 一律由 IIS/Caddy + Django FORCE_SCRIPT_NAME / request.script_name 處理
# 2) page 與 api 必須分層：
#    - page：""（入口頁）
#    - api：一律放在 "api/..." 底下，避免與 page/舊路由互相干擾
# 3) URL name 必須唯一（同 app 內不可重複），且需與 template/JS 使用的 name 完全一致
# 4) 不保留 legacy alias（避免 reverse 指到錯的 endpoint 或 name 互撞）
# ============================================================

app_name = "doc"

urlpatterns = [
    # =========================================================
    # page
    # =========================================================
    # ✅ 入口頁（統一名稱：doc_page）
    path("", views.index, name="doc_page"),

    # =========================================================
    # templates / generate（✅ 新式 API：避免與頁面/舊路由互相干擾）
    # =========================================================
    path("api/templates/", views.api_templates, name="api_templates"),
    path("api/generate/", views.api_generate, name="api_generate"),

    # =========================================================
    # attachments（✅ 新式 API）
    # =========================================================
    path("api/parse/", views.api_parse_attachments, name="api_parse_attachments"),
    path("api/parse_focus/", views.api_parse_attachments_focus, name="api_parse_attachments_focus"),

    # =========================================================
    # Sybase 來文（✅ 新式 API：路徑固定在 api/sybase/...）
    # ✅ name 採 template/JS 既用的 incoming_*，避免前後端 name 對不起來
    # =========================================================
    path("api/sybase/incoming/lookup/", views.incoming_lookup, name="incoming_lookup"),
    path("api/sybase/incoming/files/", views.incoming_files, name="incoming_files"),
    path("api/sybase/incoming/file/<str:attach_key>/", views.incoming_file, name="incoming_file"),

    # =========================================================
    # Sybase 既有公文 -> 範例庫（轉入範例）
    # =========================================================
    path("api/sybase/template/import/", views.api_import_template_from_sybase, name="api_sybase_template_import"),

    # =========================================================
    # Sybase BLOB 收納/下載（供附件重點解析與使用者下載）
    # =========================================================
    path("api/sybase/blob/stash/", api_sybase_blob_stash, name="api_sybase_blob_stash"),
    path("api/sybase/blob/download/<str:token>/", api_sybase_blob_download, name="api_sybase_blob_download"),
]

# webapps/doc/utils_login.py
from __future__ import annotations

import os
from typing import Optional, Any

from django.http import HttpRequest


def _env_bool(key: str, default: bool = False) -> bool:
    v = (os.getenv(key) or ("1" if default else "0")).strip().lower()
    return v in ("1", "true", "yes", "y", "on")


def _env_str(key: str, default: str = "") -> str:
    return (os.getenv(key) or default).strip()


def _dev_login_user() -> str:
    """
    ✅ 方案 A（本機開發用）
    - 僅在 DEBUG=1 或 DEV_LOGIN_ENABLED=1 時啟用
    - 從 DEV_LOGIN_USER 取得一個固定 IDNO
    """
    if not (_env_bool("DEBUG", False) or _env_bool("DEV_LOGIN_ENABLED", False)):
        return ""
    return _env_str("DEV_LOGIN_USER", "")


def get_effective_user(request: HttpRequest) -> Optional[Any]:
    """
    ✅ 正式切到 RemoteUser：
    - 只信任 request.user（RemoteUserMiddleware + RemoteUserBackend）
    - 若未登入，回傳 None
    """
    try:
        user = getattr(request, "user", None)
        if user and getattr(user, "is_authenticated", False):
            return user
    except Exception:
        pass
    return None


def get_login_user_idno(request: HttpRequest) -> str:
    """
    ✅ 登入者 IDNO（DB 用）
    優先順序：
    1) request.login_user（你的專案慣例，後端/DB 用）
    2) RemoteUser 的 request.user.username（fallback）
    3) ✅ DEV fallback（只在本機 / DEBUG 或 DEV_LOGIN_ENABLED）
    4) 都沒有 → ""
    """
    # 1) project convention
    try:
        v = getattr(request, "login_user", None)
        if v is not None:
            s = str(v).strip()
            if s:
                return s
    except Exception:
        pass

    # 2) RemoteUser / Django auth
    try:
        u = get_effective_user(request)
        if u is not None:
            name = getattr(u, "username", None)
            if name is not None:
                s = str(name).strip()
                if s:
                    return s
    except Exception:
        pass

    # 3) DEV fallback (local dev only)
    dev = _dev_login_user()
    if dev:
        return dev

    return ""


def get_login_user_name(request: HttpRequest) -> str:
    """
    ✅ 顯示用姓名（UI 用）
    優先順序：
    1) request.login_user_name（middleware 已算好的就直接用）
    2) Oracle 查姓名（若 oracle_emp 有提供 timeout+cache 版本，這裡會很穩）
    3) fallback 用 IDNO
    """
    # 1) middleware already set
    try:
        n = getattr(request, "login_user_name", None)
        if n is not None:
            s = str(n).strip()
            if s:
                return s
    except Exception:
        pass

    # 2) oracle lookup (optional)
    emp_id = get_login_user_idno(request)
    if not emp_id:
        return ""

    try:
        from webapps.portal.oracle_emp import get_emp_name  # lazy import
        name = (get_emp_name(emp_id) or "").strip()
        if name:
            return name
    except Exception:
        pass

    # 3) fallback
    return emp_id

# webapps/doc/views_generate.py
from __future__ import annotations

import json
import os
from typing import Any, Dict, Optional

from django.http import HttpRequest, JsonResponse
from django.views.decorators.csrf import csrf_exempt

from webapps.portal.decorators import require_node
from webapps.doc.models import DocumentTemplate
from webapps.doc.prompt import build_prompt as build_prompt_v2
from webapps.llm.llm_factory import get_chat_model

from webapps.doc.views_helpers import (
    _safe_str,
    _env_bool,
    _to_text,
    _clean_generated_draft,
    _clean_tags,
    _infer_tags_from_text,
    _valid_doc_types_set,
    _templates_visibility_filter,
    _first_subject_line,
    _build_seed_title,
    _build_seed_description,
    _draft_to_sections,
    _normalize_doc_fields,
    _postprocess_official_style,
    _save_template_with_conflict_policy_v2,
)

# ✅ RAG: context retrieval (Chroma knowledge base)
try:
    from webapps.llm.services import LLMServiceConfig, try_get_rag_context
    _RAG_SERVICES_OK = True
except Exception:
    LLMServiceConfig = None  # type: ignore
    try_get_rag_context = None  # type: ignore
    _RAG_SERVICES_OK = False


@csrf_exempt
@require_node("doc", api=True)
def api_generate(request: HttpRequest):
    if request.method != "POST":
        return JsonResponse({"ok": False, "error": "method not allowed"}, status=405)

    try:
        body = json.loads(request.body.decode("utf-8"))
    except Exception:
        return JsonResponse({"ok": False, "error": "invalid json"}, status=400)

    user = getattr(request, "user", None)
    is_auth = bool(user and getattr(user, "is_authenticated", False))
    valid_doc_types = _valid_doc_types_set()

    doc_type = _safe_str(body.get("doc_type")).strip()
    requirement = _safe_str(body.get("requirement")).strip()
    example_ids = body.get("example_ids", []) or []
    reference_text = _safe_str(body.get("reference_text")).strip()
    incoming_text = _safe_str(body.get("incoming_text")).strip()
    attachments_text = _safe_str(body.get("attachments_text")).strip()

    save_as_template = bool(body.get("save_as_template", False))
    draft_to_save = _safe_str(body.get("draft_to_save")).strip()

    seed_title = _safe_str(body.get("seed_title")).strip()
    seed_description = _safe_str(body.get("seed_description")).strip()
    seed_tags = body.get("seed_tags", None)
    seed_doc_fields = body.get("seed_doc_fields", None)

    save_scope = (_safe_str(body.get("save_scope") or "personal").strip().lower() or "personal")
    if save_scope not in ("public", "personal"):
        save_scope = "personal"

    save_on_conflict = (_safe_str(body.get("save_on_conflict") or "suffix").strip().lower() or "suffix")
    if save_on_conflict not in ("overwrite", "suffix"):
        save_on_conflict = "suffix"

    if save_as_template and save_scope == "personal" and (not is_auth):
        return JsonResponse({"ok": False, "error": "login required for personal templates"}, status=401)

    if not doc_type or doc_type not in valid_doc_types:
        return JsonResponse({"ok": False, "error": "doc_type is required and must be valid"}, status=400)

    if not isinstance(example_ids, list):
        return JsonResponse({"ok": False, "error": "example_ids must be a list"}, status=400)

    if not requirement and not (save_as_template and draft_to_save):
        return JsonResponse({"ok": False, "error": "requirement is required"}, status=400)

    example_qs = DocumentTemplate.objects.filter(
        id__in=example_ids,
        doc_type=doc_type,
    )
    example_qs = _templates_visibility_filter(example_qs, user=user, is_auth=is_auth)
    examples = list(example_qs.values_list("content_text", flat=True))

    rag_backend = "rag_disabled"
    rag_query = ""
    if _RAG_SERVICES_OK and _env_bool("DOC_RAG_ENABLED", True):
        try:
            rag_query = "\n".join(
                [
                    f"公文類型：{doc_type}",
                    f"撰擬需求：{requirement}",
                    f"來文/背景：{incoming_text}",
                    f"附件摘錄：{attachments_text}",
                ]
            ).strip()

            rag_cfg = LLMServiceConfig(
                rag_k=int(os.getenv("DOC_RAG_K", "4")),
            )

            rag_context, rag_backend = try_get_rag_context(rag_query, config=rag_cfg)

            if rag_context:
                max_chars = int(os.getenv("DOC_RAG_MAX_CHARS", "4000"))
                if len(rag_context) > max_chars:
                    rag_context = rag_context[:max_chars] + "\n（以下略）"

                reference_text = (
                    "【RAG 知識庫檢索參考】\n"
                    + rag_context.strip()
                    + "\n\n"
                    + "【使用者提供參考】\n"
                    + (reference_text.strip() if reference_text else "（無）")
                ).strip()

        except Exception:
            rag_backend = "rag_inject_error"

    prompt = build_prompt_v2(
        doc_type=doc_type,
        requirement=requirement,
        examples=examples,
        reference_text=reference_text,
        incoming_text=incoming_text,
        attachments_text=attachments_text,
    )

    def _save_sections_as_template(draft_text: str, draft_sections: Dict[str, Any]) -> int:
        if seed_tags is None:
            tags = _infer_tags_from_text(draft_text)
        else:
            tags = _clean_tags(seed_tags)

        title = seed_title or _build_seed_title(doc_type, draft_text)
        description = seed_description or _build_seed_description(doc_type, tags, draft_text)

        doc_fields = _normalize_doc_fields(seed_doc_fields)
        meta = {"source": "generated", "rag_backend": rag_backend}

        obj, created, final_title, policy, status_msg = _save_template_with_conflict_policy_v2(
            title=title,
            doc_type=doc_type,
            description=description,
            sections=draft_sections,
            doc_fields=doc_fields,
            meta=meta,
            tags=tags,
            scope=save_scope,
            user=user,
            on_conflict=save_on_conflict,
            schema_ver=2,
            max_suffix_try=int(os.getenv("DOC_TPL_SUFFIX_MAX_TRY", "50")),
        )
        return obj.id

    # ✅ 只存入範例（不生成）
    if save_as_template and draft_to_save:
        try:
            draft_clean = _clean_generated_draft(draft_to_save)
            draft_clean = _postprocess_official_style(draft_clean)
            if not draft_clean.strip():
                raise ValueError("draft_to_save is empty after cleaning")

            draft_sections = _draft_to_sections(doc_type, draft_clean)
            if not draft_sections:
                raise ValueError("cannot parse draft_to_save into sections")

            saved_template_id = _save_sections_as_template(draft_clean, draft_sections)

            return JsonResponse(
                {
                    "ok": True,
                    "draft_text": draft_clean,
                    "draft_sections": draft_sections,
                    "prompt": prompt,
                    "rag_backend": rag_backend,
                    "rag_query": rag_query,
                    "meta": {
                        "example_ids": example_ids,
                        "examples_used": len(examples),
                        "saved_template_id": saved_template_id,
                    },
                },
                status=200,
            )
        except Exception as e:
            return JsonResponse(
                {"ok": False, "error": str(e), "prompt": prompt, "rag_backend": rag_backend, "rag_query": rag_query},
                status=500,
            )

    # ✅ 正常生成
    try:
        llm = get_chat_model()  # ✅ LLM_FACTORY only
        draft_raw = _to_text(llm.invoke(prompt)).strip() or "(模型未回傳內容)"
        draft_text = _clean_generated_draft(draft_raw)
        draft_text = _postprocess_official_style(draft_text)

        draft_sections = _draft_to_sections(doc_type, draft_text)

        model_type = (os.getenv("MODEL_TYPE") or "AUTO").strip().upper()
        provider = "openai" if model_type == "OPENAI" else ("ollama" if model_type == "OLLAMA" else "auto")
        model = (
            (os.getenv("OPENAI_MODEL") or "").strip()
            if provider == "openai"
            else ((os.getenv("OLLAMA_LLM_MODEL") or "").strip() or (os.getenv("OLLAMA_MODEL") or "").strip())
        ) or "unknown"

        saved_template_id: Optional[int] = None
        if save_as_template and not draft_to_save:
            if save_scope == "personal" and (not is_auth):
                return JsonResponse({"ok": False, "error": "login required for personal templates"}, status=401)

            if not draft_sections:
                draft_sections = {"subject": _first_subject_line(draft_text) or "（未提供主旨）", "explain": draft_text}

            saved_template_id = _save_sections_as_template(draft_text, draft_sections)

        return JsonResponse(
            {
                "ok": True,
                "draft_text": draft_text,
                "draft_sections": draft_sections,
                "prompt": prompt,
                "provider": provider,
                "model": model,
                "rag_backend": rag_backend,
                "rag_query": rag_query,
                "meta": {
                    "example_ids": example_ids,
                    "examples_used": len(examples),
                    "saved_template_id": saved_template_id,
                },
            },
            status=200,
        )

    except Exception as e:
        return JsonResponse(
            {"ok": False, "error": str(e), "prompt": prompt, "rag_backend": rag_backend, "rag_query": rag_query},
            status=500,
        )



===== 文件: H:\AI\AI_TOOLS\webapps\doc\views_helpers.py =====
=== 代碼內容 ===
# webapps/doc/views_helpers.py
from __future__ import annotations

import os
import re
from typing import Any, Dict, List, Optional, Tuple

from django.db import connection as dj_connection, transaction
from django.db.models import Q
from django.db.utils import IntegrityError, OperationalError, NotSupportedError

from webapps.doc.models import DocumentTemplate


# ============================================================
# helpers
# ============================================================

def _safe_str(x: Any) -> str:
    return "" if x is None else str(x)


def _env_bool(name: str, default: bool = False) -> bool:
    v = (os.getenv(name, str(int(default))) or "").strip().lower()
    return v in ("1", "true", "yes", "y", "on")


def _to_text(x: Any) -> str:
    if x is None:
        return ""
    if hasattr(x, "content"):
        return getattr(x, "content") or ""
    if isinstance(x, dict):
        if "content" in x:
            return str(x.get("content") or "")
        if "text" in x:
            return str(x.get("text") or "")
    return str(x)


def _clean_generated_draft(text: str) -> str:
    s = (text or "").lstrip()
    s = s.lstrip("\ufeff").lstrip()

    # 去掉模型可能吐出的 tags/說明頭
    s = re.sub(
        r'^\s*[（(][\s\S]{0,600}?\btags\s*:\s*[\s\S]{0,300}?[）)]\s*\r?\n',
        "",
        s,
        flags=re.IGNORECASE,
    )
    s = re.sub(
        r"^\s*[（(]?\s*tags\s*:\s*.*?[）)]?\s*\r?\n",
        "",
        s,
        flags=re.IGNORECASE,
    )
    s = re.sub(r"^\s*[（(].{0,120}[）)]\s*\r?\n", "", s)
    return s.lstrip()


def _clean_tags(tags: Any) -> List[str]:
    if tags is None:
        return []
    if not isinstance(tags, list):
        return []
    out: List[str] = []
    seen = set()
    for x in tags:
        s = _safe_str(x).strip()
        if s and s not in seen:
            seen.add(s)
            out.append(s)
    return out


def _infer_tags_from_text(text: str) -> List[str]:
    t = (text or "")
    rules: List[Tuple[str, str]] = [
        ("資訊", "系統|資安|弱點|帳號|權限|伺服器|備份|機房|端點|EDR|SOC|告警|監測|MES|IIoT"),
        ("採購", "採購|招標|詢價|契約|廠商|決標|開標|比價|規格|驗收|開口|框架"),
        ("主財", "預算|經費|核銷|報支|憑證|請款|撥款|付款|概算|決算"),
        ("品保", "品質|檢驗|首件|不良|異常|RCA|稽核|改善|報廢"),
        ("生產", "產線|稼動|排程|產能|備料|出貨|停線|試量產"),
        ("設施供應", "修繕|空調|電力|消防|水電|工程|設備保養|維護|治具"),
        ("人事", "人力|招募|派遣|約用|教育訓練|考績"),
        ("行政", "會議|公告|制度|流程|總務|庶務|文書"),
        ("研發", "研發|設計|驗證|試驗|專利|新產品"),
        ("計劃", "計畫|專案|里程碑|年度計畫"),
        ("職安衛", "職安|工安|環安|安全衛生|危害|風險"),
        ("測情", "情資|研判|通報|預警|態勢|威脅"),
    ]

    out: List[str] = []
    for tag, pattern in rules:
        if re.search(pattern, t):
            out.append(tag)

    seen = set()
    dedup: List[str] = []
    for x in out:
        if x not in seen:
            seen.add(x)
            dedup.append(x)
    return dedup


# ============================================================
# ✅ doc_type choices helpers
# ============================================================

def _doc_type_choices_dict() -> Dict[str, str]:
    """
    不要用 DocumentTemplate.DOC_TYPE_CHOICES（有些專案 models 沒掛 class attribute）
    這裡用 Django field choices 取得，最穩。
    """
    try:
        field = DocumentTemplate._meta.get_field("doc_type")
        return {str(k): str(v) for k, v in (field.choices or [])}
    except Exception:
        return {}


def _valid_doc_types_set() -> set:
    return set(_doc_type_choices_dict().keys())


def _doc_type_label(doc_type: str) -> str:
    return _doc_type_choices_dict().get(doc_type, doc_type)


def _first_subject_line(draft: str) -> str:
    """
    從草稿中抓第一個「主旨：...」
    抓不到就回空字串
    """
    for line in (draft or "").splitlines():
        t = line.strip()
        if not t:
            continue
        m = re.match(r"^主旨[:：]\s*(.+)$", t)
        if m:
            return m.group(1).strip()
    return ""


def _build_seed_title(doc_type: str, draft: str) -> str:
    label = _doc_type_label(doc_type)
    subj = _first_subject_line(draft) or "未命名範例"
    subj = re.sub(r"[。．\.]+$", "", subj).strip()
    if len(subj) > 40:
        subj = subj[:40] + "…"
    return f"{label}—{subj}範例"


def _build_seed_description(doc_type: str, tags: List[str], draft: str) -> str:
    parts = []
    if tags:
        parts.append(" / ".join(tags[:4]))
    subj = _first_subject_line(draft)
    if subj:
        subj = subj.strip()
        if len(subj) > 28:
            subj = subj[:28] + "…"
        parts.append(subj)
    return " / ".join([p for p in parts if p]).strip() or "自動產生範例"


# ============================================================
# ✅ Visibility（正式登入：public + owner personal；未登入：只 public）
# ============================================================

def _templates_visibility_filter(qs, *, user, is_auth: bool):
    """
    - 已登入：public + personal(owner=user)
    - 未登入：public
    """
    if is_auth:
        return qs.filter(Q(scope="public") | Q(scope="personal", owner=user))
    return qs.filter(scope="public")


def _apply_tag_filter(qs, tag: str):
    """
    支援 QuerySet / list
    - SQLite：JSONField contains 不支援 -> Python filter（回傳 list）
    - 非 SQLite：優先 tags__contains=[tag]，失敗再 Python filter
    """
    tag = (tag or "").strip()
    if not tag:
        return qs

    def _py_filter(iterable):
        return [t for t in iterable if tag in (getattr(t, "tags", None) or [])]

    if dj_connection.vendor == "sqlite":
        try:
            qs = qs.order_by("-created_at")
        except Exception:
            qs = qs.order_by("-id")
        return _py_filter(qs)

    try:
        return qs.filter(tags__contains=[tag])
    except (NotSupportedError, OperationalError):
        return _py_filter(qs)


# ============================================================
# ✅ 公文修辭標準化（表格式 rules + 迴圈，好維護）
# ============================================================

_PHRASE_RULES: List[Dict[str, Any]] = [
    {"mode": "replace", "src": "敬請核示。", "dst": "請核示。"},
    {"mode": "replace", "src": "敬請核示", "dst": "請核示"},
    {"mode": "replace", "src": "敬請查照。", "dst": "請查照。"},
    {"mode": "replace", "src": "敬請查照", "dst": "請查照"},
    {"mode": "replace", "src": "敬請鑒核。", "dst": "請鑒核。"},
    {"mode": "replace", "src": "敬請鑒核", "dst": "請鑒核"},
    {"mode": "replace", "src": "敬請惠復。", "dst": "請惠復。"},
    {"mode": "replace", "src": "敬請惠復", "dst": "請惠復"},
    {"mode": "replace", "src": "敬請照辦。", "dst": "請照辦。"},
    {"mode": "replace", "src": "敬請照辦", "dst": "請照辦"},
    {"mode": "replace", "src": "敬請轉知。", "dst": "請轉知。"},
    {"mode": "replace", "src": "敬請轉知", "dst": "請轉知"},
    {"mode": "replace", "src": "敬請配合。", "dst": "請配合辦理。"},
    {"mode": "replace", "src": "敬請配合", "dst": "請配合辦理"},
    {"mode": "replace", "src": "敬請見復。", "dst": "請見復。"},
    {"mode": "replace", "src": "敬請見復", "dst": "請見復"},
]


def _apply_phrase_rules(text: str) -> str:
    t = text or ""
    for r in _PHRASE_RULES:
        mode = r.get("mode")
        if mode == "replace":
            t = t.replace(r.get("src", ""), r.get("dst", ""))
        elif mode == "regex":
            pat = r.get("pattern", "")
            repl = r.get("repl", "")
            flags = r.get("flags", 0)
            if pat:
                t = re.sub(pat, repl, t, flags=flags)
    return t


def _merge_standalone_courtesy_line(text: str) -> str:
    """
    ✅ 避免「請核示。」等獨立成行，合併到上一行末尾
    """
    lines = (text or "").splitlines()
    if not lines:
        return text or ""

    courtesy_set = {
        "請核示。", "請核示",
        "請查照。", "請查照",
        "請鑒核。", "請鑒核",
        "請惠復。", "請惠復",
        "請照辦。", "請照辦",
        "請轉知。", "請轉知",
        "請配合辦理。", "請配合辦理",
    }

    out: List[str] = []
    for raw in lines:
        line = raw.rstrip()
        s = line.strip()

        if not s:
            out.append(line)
            continue

        if s in courtesy_set and out:
            j = len(out) - 1
            while j >= 0 and not out[j].strip():
                j -= 1
            if j >= 0:
                prev = out[j].rstrip()

                if s.replace("。", "") in prev:
                    continue

                if prev.endswith("。"):
                    prev2 = prev[:-1] + "，" + (s if s.endswith("。") else s + "。")
                elif prev.endswith(("；", "，", ",", "：", ":", "、")):
                    prev2 = prev + (s if s.endswith("。") else s + "。")
                else:
                    prev2 = prev + "，" + (s if s.endswith("。") else s + "。")

                out[j] = prev2
                continue

        out.append(line)

    while out and not out[-1].strip():
        out.pop()

    return "\n".join(out)


def _postprocess_official_style(text: str) -> str:
    t = (text or "").strip()
    if not t:
        return t
    t = _apply_phrase_rules(t)
    t = _merge_standalone_courtesy_line(t)
    return t.strip()


# ============================================================
# New schema helpers (sections/doc_fields)
# ============================================================

def _extract_section_blocks(text: str) -> Dict[str, str]:
    src = (text or "").strip()
    if not src:
        return {}

    src = src.replace("：", ":")

    labels = ["主旨:", "說明:", "擬辦:", "辦法:", "附件:", "施行:", "生效:", "配合:", "結語:"]
    pattern = r"(?m)^(%s)\s*" % "|".join([re.escape(x) for x in labels])

    hits = list(re.finditer(pattern, src))
    if not hits:
        return {}

    blocks: List[Tuple[str, int, int]] = []
    for i, m in enumerate(hits):
        start = m.start()
        end = hits[i + 1].start() if i + 1 < len(hits) else len(src)
        label = m.group(1).strip()
        blocks.append((label, start, end))

    out: Dict[str, str] = {}
    for label, start, end in blocks:
        seg = src[start:end].strip()
        seg = re.sub(r"^%s\s*" % re.escape(label), "", seg, flags=re.IGNORECASE).strip()

        if label.startswith("主旨"):
            out["subject"] = seg
        elif label.startswith("說明"):
            out["explain"] = seg
        elif label.startswith("擬辦") or label.startswith("辦法") or label.startswith("配合"):
            out["method"] = seg
        elif label.startswith("附件"):
            out["attachments"] = seg
        elif label.startswith("施行") or label.startswith("生效"):
            out["enforce"] = seg
        elif label.startswith("結語"):
            out["closing"] = seg

    return {k: v for k, v in out.items() if (v or "").strip()}


def _draft_to_sections(doc_type: str, draft_text: str) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    dt = (doc_type or "").strip()
    txt = (draft_text or "").strip()
    if not txt:
        return {}

    if dt == "note":
        title = _first_subject_line(txt) or ""
        points: List[str] = []
        action = ""

        for line in txt.splitlines():
            t = line.strip()
            if not t:
                continue
            if re.match(r"^主旨[:：]", t):
                continue
            if re.match(r"^[•\-\*]\s+", t) or re.match(r"^\d+\.\s+", t):
                points.append(re.sub(r"^[•\-\*]\s+|\d+\.\s+", "", t).strip())
            if re.match(r"^(擬辦|請示)[:：]", t):
                action = re.sub(r"^(擬辦|請示)[:：]\s*", "", t).strip()

        sections: Dict[str, Any] = {
            "title": title or "便籤",
            "points": [p for p in points if p],
        }
        if action:
            sections["action"] = action
        return sections

    sec = _extract_section_blocks(txt)

    if not sec:
        lines = [l.strip() for l in txt.splitlines() if l.strip()]
        if not lines:
            return {}
        sec = {
            "subject": lines[0],
            "explain": "\n".join(lines[1:]).strip() if len(lines) > 1 else "",
        }

    if dt == "order_draft":
        out: Dict[str, Any] = {
            "subject": sec.get("subject", ""),
            "explain": sec.get("explain", ""),
        }
        if sec.get("enforce"):
            out["enforce"] = sec.get("enforce", "")
        if sec.get("attachments"):
            out["attachments"] = sec.get("attachments", "")
        if not out.get("enforce") and sec.get("method"):
            out["enforce"] = sec.get("method", "")
        return {k: v for k, v in out.items() if (str(v).strip())}

    out2: Dict[str, Any] = {
        "subject": sec.get("subject", ""),
        "explain": sec.get("explain", ""),
    }
    if sec.get("method"):
        out2["method"] = sec.get("method", "")
    if sec.get("attachments"):
        out2["attachments"] = sec.get("attachments", "")
    if dt == "letter_draft":
        if sec.get("closing"):
            out2["closing"] = sec.get("closing", "")
    return {k: v for k, v in out2.items() if (str(v).strip())}


def _normalize_sections(body_sections: Any) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    if isinstance(body_sections, dict):
        out: Dict[str, Any] = {}
        for k, v in body_sections.items():
            if v is None:
                continue
            if isinstance(v, (dict, list)):
                out[k] = v
            else:
                out[k] = str(v)
        return out
    return {}


def _normalize_doc_fields(body_fields: Any) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    return body_fields if isinstance(body_fields, dict) else {}


def _normalize_meta(body_meta: Any) -> Dict[str, Any]:
    return body_meta if isinstance(body_meta, dict) else {}


def _unique_lookup_for_scope(*, scope: str, user, title: str) -> dict:
    if scope == "public":
        return {"scope": "public", "title": title}
    return {"scope": "personal", "owner": user, "title": title}


def _save_template_with_conflict_policy_v2(
    *,
    title: str,
    doc_type: str,
    description: str,
    sections: Dict[str, Any],
    doc_fields: Dict[str, Any],
    meta: Dict[str, Any],
    tags: List[str],
    scope: str,
    user,
    on_conflict: str,
    schema_ver: int = 2,
    max_suffix_try: int = 50,
):
    on_conflict = (on_conflict or "suffix").strip().lower()
    if on_conflict not in ("overwrite", "suffix"):
        on_conflict = "suffix"

    defaults = {
        "doc_type": doc_type,
        "description": description,
        "sections": sections,
        "doc_fields": doc_fields,
        "meta": meta,
        "schema_ver": schema_ver,
        "tags": tags,
        "scope": scope,
        "owner": (user if scope == "personal" else None),
    }

    if on_conflict == "overwrite":
        lookup = _unique_lookup_for_scope(scope=scope, user=user, title=title)
        old = DocumentTemplate.objects.filter(**lookup).first()
        if old:
            if (old.sections or {}) == (sections or {}):
                return old, False, old.title, "overwrite", "skipped_same_sections"

        obj, created = DocumentTemplate.objects.update_or_create(defaults=defaults, **lookup)
        return obj, created, obj.title, "overwrite", "saved"

    base = title
    for n in range(1, max_suffix_try + 1):
        try_title = base if n == 1 else f"{base}（{n}）"
        try:
            with transaction.atomic():
                obj = DocumentTemplate.objects.create(
                    title=try_title,
                    doc_type=doc_type,
                    description=description,
                    sections=sections,
                    doc_fields=doc_fields,
                    meta=meta,
                    schema_ver=schema_ver,
                    tags=tags,
                    scope=scope,
                    owner=(user if scope == "personal" else None),
                )
            return obj, True, obj.title, "suffix", "saved"
        except IntegrityError:
            continue

    raise ValueError("title conflict: too many duplicates, please change title")


# ============================================================
# File extractors (DOCX / ODT / PDF)
# ============================================================

def _extract_text_docx(file_obj) -> str:
    from docx import Document
    doc = Document(file_obj)
    lines = []
    for p in doc.paragraphs:
        t = (p.text or "").strip()
        if t:
            lines.append(t)
    return "\n".join(lines)


def _extract_text_odt(file_obj) -> str:
    from odf.opendocument import load
    from odf import text as odf_text

    odt = load(file_obj)
    lines = []
    for p in odt.getElementsByType(odf_text.P):
        t = "".join([n.data for n in p.childNodes if getattr(n, "data", None)])
        t = (t or "").strip()
        if t:
            lines.append(t)
    return "\n".join(lines)


def _extract_text_pdf(file_obj) -> str:
    from pypdf import PdfReader
    reader = PdfReader(file_obj)
    lines = []
    for page in reader.pages:
        t = (page.extract_text() or "").strip()
        if t:
            lines.append(t)
    return "\n\n".join(lines)


def _extract_text_by_ext(file_obj, filename: str) -> str:
    ext = os.path.splitext(filename.lower())[1]
    if ext == ".docx":
        return _extract_text_docx(file_obj)
    if ext in (".odt",):
        return _extract_text_odt(file_obj)
    if ext == ".pdf":
        return _extract_text_pdf(file_obj)
    raise ValueError(f"unsupported file type: {ext}")


# ============================================================
# parse_focus prompt helpers
# ============================================================

def _build_attach_focus_prompt(combined_text: str, extra_hint: str = "") -> str:
    extra_hint = (extra_hint or "").strip()

    return f"""
你是公文助理。請以「繁體中文」輸出，並且只輸出「純文字」。
禁止輸出 HTML、禁止輸出 Markdown、禁止輸出任何 <tag> 或 ```。

你會收到「附件轉文字內容」（可能包含多份附件）。
請整理成「擬案依據（附件）重點摘要」。

【輸出格式（必須照做）】
重點1：...
重點2：...
重點3：...
（最多 12 點；每點一行；內容務必精煉）

【整理規則】
1) 只根據內容整理重點，不得臆測、不捏造日期/金額/單位/人名。
2) 優先整理：背景/需求/現況/問題/風險/建議作法/期程/附件提及的規格或關鍵條件。
3) 若內容不足，請照格式輸出：
重點1：資料不足，缺少（...）
重點2：資料不足，缺少（...）

【使用者補充提示（若有）】
{extra_hint if extra_hint else "（無）"}

【附件轉文字內容】
{combined_text}
""".strip()


def _ensure_focus_numbered(text: str, max_points: int = 12) -> str:
    """
    保險：把模型輸出盡量整理成
    重點1：...
    重點2：...
    """
    s = (text or "").strip()
    if not s:
        return ""

    if re.search(r"(?m)^重點\s*\d+\s*[:：]", s):
        return s

    lines = [ln.strip() for ln in s.splitlines() if ln.strip()]
    if not lines:
        return ""

    if len(lines) == 1:
        tmp = re.split(r"[。；;\n\r]+", lines[0])
        lines = [x.strip() for x in tmp if x.strip()]

    lines = lines[:max_points]
    out = []
    for i, ln in enumerate(lines, 1):
        out.append(f"重點{i}：{ln}")
    return "\n".join(out).strip()

# webapps/doc/views_pages.py
from __future__ import annotations

from django.http import HttpRequest
from django.shortcuts import render

from webapps.portal.decorators import require_node


def _norm_base(p: str) -> str:
    s = (p or "").strip()
    if not s:
        return ""
    if not s.startswith("/"):
        s = "/" + s
    while len(s) > 1 and s.endswith("/"):
        s = s[:-1]
    return "" if s == "/" else s


@require_node("doc")
def index(request: HttpRequest):
    """
    規範重點（Mandatory）
    1) 前端 baseUrl 只能讀 body[data-base-url]（template 注入）
    2) baseUrl 必須是「proxy prefix + app mount」，不得只給 request.script_name
       - 例：/doc 或 /djangoai/doc 或 /comment/doc
    3) views 不做任何前端路由推導；只負責注入正確 baseUrl 字串
    """
    # request.script_name：反代 prefix（可能為 /djangoai 或 /comment 或空）
    script = _norm_base(getattr(request, "script_name", "") or request.META.get("SCRIPT_NAME", ""))

    # request.path_info：Django 內部路徑（此頁通常是 /）
    path_info = (request.path_info or "/").strip()
    if not path_info.startswith("/"):
        path_info = "/" + path_info
    # 入口頁 / → 代表「doc 的 mount root」
    mount = "/doc" if path_info == "/" else path_info.rstrip("/")

    app_base_url = _norm_base((script + mount).replace("//", "/"))

    return render(
        request,
        "doc/index.html",
        {
            # index.html 用：<body data-base-url="{{ app_base_url }}">
            "app_base_url": app_base_url,
        },
    )
